<p>by <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/autocad/fenton-webb.html">Fenton Webb</a></p>  <p>I’m presenting a class on the new security features inside of AutoCAD 2014 at this years AU – classes <a href="https://events.au.autodesk.com/content/">DV3456</a> (Lecture) and <a href="https://events.au.autodesk.com/content/">DV3459-R</a> (Round table after-lecture discussion). I thought you might like to see my handout document in advance, let me know if you don’t follow anything and I’ll try to explain/update the document for you…</p>  <h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: ; mso-ansi-language: en-us"><font face="Cambria"><font style="font-size: 13pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">The Original Security Problem</font></font></font></span></h2>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000"></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Back in the AutoCAD 2012 time frame a problem AutoCAD arose with people exploiting the LISP auto loading mechanism used by acad.lsp acaddoc.lsp/fas/vlx files to infect user’s machines with viruses. We published a Technical Solution to address a variation of the virus <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;</span></font><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/getdoc/id=TS13717811"><font color="#0000ff">http://usa.autodesk.com/getdoc/id=TS13717811</font></a><font color="#000000"> </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">At that time, AutoCAD would autoload the first acad/acaddoc/acad20xx/acad20xxdoc. lsp/fas/vlx or acad.dvb file it encountered in its AutoCAD Support File Search path. All the AutoCAD viruses out there were exploiting this single feature.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>We decided to provide an option to disable this feature since most, if not all, users use only a single acad.lsp, acaddoc.lsp or acad.dvb.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Most of these viruses used to get to a user by slipping the lisp files into a zip file containing legitimate drawings. When a user unzips the zip file and double clicks on a drawing file to open it, the lisp files get loaded and infect the machine.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">There are 3 different groups of these types of user created startup files:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 39.15pt; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">1.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">acad.lsp/fas/vlx </span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 39.15pt; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">2.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">acaddoc.lsp/fas/vlx </span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 39.15pt; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo1"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">3.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">acad.dvb</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">FAS &amp; VLX filetypes are compiled LSP files.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>DVB is a Visual Basic for Applications macro file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">In addition, we sometimes used to ship acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp files (xx represents the release year). These files are “reserved” for AutoCAD use only.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Only 1 of each group is loaded.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">If acad.lsp, acad.fas and acad.vlx are all present in the same directory, only acad.vlx is loaded and acad.fas and acad.lsp is ignored. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">If all 7 files are present, only acad.vlx, acaddoc.vlx and acad.dvb are loaded.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>But it depends on which directory these files are found.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Each of these files are loaded from the first place AutoCAD finds them as it works through its search path. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">The search path isn’t just what is defined in the Options Files tab; it also includes the current folder (usually the start-in folder defined in the program shortcut) and the current drawing’s folder. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">The current folder is searched first, then the drawing folder, then the rest of the search path. So if acad.lsp is found first, it will get loaded even if an acad.fas/vlx exists.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>(At any time only 1 of the files acad.lsp, acad.vlx or acad.fas are loaded, even when the files are located in different directories. If AutoCAD finds and loads one of these files, it stops looking for the other 2).</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">The Search order for these files is:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo2"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">1.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">Acad.VLX</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo2"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">2.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">Acad.FAS</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo2"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: x-none"><span style="mso-list: ignore">3.<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none">Acad.LSP</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">But if all 3 (or 2) of the files are present in a directory, AutoCAD first checks if the .lsp file is newer than the .VLX or the .FAS file. If it is, then AutoCAD loads the .LSP file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Acad.lsp/fas/vlx, acaddoc.lsp/fas/vlx or acad.dvb are not shipped with AutoCAD, and are created by users.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">The reserved acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp files were installed in the &lt;installdir&gt;\support folder.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>(As of AutoCAD 2013, the acad20xxdoc.lsp file is installed into a localized sub-folder such as en-us). acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp were supposed to be for AutoCAD internal use only, so users should not have been creating/editing them. We clearly documented this in the Help documentation. But we were treating these files like acad.lsp and acaddoc.lsp (i.e. the first file found in the search path is autoloaded). </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">One of our CAD bloggers documents the order in which these files are loaded- Section B in </font><a href="http://www.blog.cadnauseam.com/2008/09/01/what-is-loaded-at-autocad-startup-and-when/"><font color="#0000ff">http://www.blog.cadnauseam.com/2008/09/01/what-is-loaded-at-autocad-startup-and-when/</font></a><font color="#000000"> If all these files are found, AutoCAD will load all of them. (The only exception is when all 3 versions (i.e acad.lsp, acad.vlx and acad.fas are found in a directory, only acad.lsp is loaded – the other 2 are ignored). </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 14pt; mso-fareast-language: x-none; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 12pt" color="#000000">References</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">How to detect and remove the Acad.vlx virus:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=13717811&amp;linkID=9240617"><font color="#0000ff">http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=13717811&amp;linkID=9240617</font></a><font color="#000000"> </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Comparing the acad*.lsp files:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=2897258&amp;linkID=9240617"><font color="#0000ff">http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=2897258&amp;linkID=9240617</font></a><font color="#000000"> </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">What is loaded at AutoCAD startup, and when?:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font><a href="http://www.blog.cadnauseam.com/2008/09/01/what-is-loaded-at-autocad-startup-and-when/"><font color="#0000ff">http://www.blog.cadnauseam.com/2008/09/01/what-is-loaded-at-autocad-startup-and-when/</font></a><font color="#000000"> </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-language: x-none"><font color="#000000">Comparing the acad*.lsp files:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=2897258&amp;linkID=9240617"><font color="#0000ff">http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/ps/dl/item?siteID=123112&amp;id=2897258&amp;linkID=9240617</font></a><font color="#000000"> </font></span></p>  <h3 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="X-NONE" style="color: "><font face="Cambria"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">&#160;</font></font></font></span></h3>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 14pt; mso-fareast-language: x-none; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 12pt" color="#000000">Additional Information from the Help docs</font></span></b><span lang="X-NONE" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-ansi-language: x-none; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-fareast-language: x-none; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-bidi-font-style: italic"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Help-&gt;Customization Guide-&gt; </font><a href="http://exchange.autodesk.com/autocad/enu/online-help/search#WS73099cc142f4875513fb5cd10c4aa30d6b-7f79.htm"><font color="#0000ff">The ACAD.LSP File</font></a></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">You can create an acad.lsp file if you regularly use specific AutoLISP routines. When you start AutoCAD, it searches the support file search path for an acad.lsp file. If an acad.lsp file is found, it is loaded into memory. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial">Warning: </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial">Do not modify the reserved acad2012.lsp file. Autodesk provides the acad2012.lsp file, which contains AutoLISP defined functions that are required by AutoCAD. This file is loaded into memory immediately before the acad.lsp file is loaded.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Help-&gt;Customization Guide-&gt; </font><a href="http://exchange.autodesk.com/autocad/enu/online-help/search%23WS73099cc142f4875513fb5cd10c4aa30d6b-7f72.htm"><font color="#0000ff">The ACADDOC.LSP File</font></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">Most users will have a single <i>acaddoc.lsp</i> file for all document-based AutoLISP routines. AutoCAD searches for an<i>acaddoc.lsp</i> file in the order defined by the library path; therefore, with this feature, you can have a different <i>acaddoc.lsp</i>file in each drawing directory, which would load specific AutoLISP routines for certain types of drawings or jobs.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: "></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial">Warning: </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial">Do not modify the reserved <i>acad2012doc</i>.<i>lsp</i> file. Autodesk provides the <i>acad2012doc</i>.<i>lsp</i> file, which contains AutoLISP-defined functions that are required by AutoCAD. This file is loaded into memory immediately before the <i>acaddoc.lsp</i> file is loaded.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Help-&gt;Customization Guide-&gt; </font><a href="http://exchange.autodesk.com/autocad/enu/online-help/search#WS73099cc142f4875513fb5cd10c4aa30d6b-7f97.htm"><font color="#0000ff">Automatically Load and Execute VBA Projects</font></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: calibri"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">The <i>acad</i>.<i>dvb</i> file is useful if you want to load a specific VBA project that contains macros you want each time you start AutoCAD. Each time you start a new AutoCAD drawing session, AutoCAD searches for the <i>acad</i>.<i>dvb</i> file and loads it.</font></span></p>  <h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: ; mso-ansi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold" size="2">&#160;</font></font></span></h2>  <h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: ; mso-ansi-language: en-us"><font face="Cambria"><font style="font-size: 13pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">The Solution – AutoCAD 2012 sp1</font></font></font></span><span lang="X-NONE" style="color: "></span></h2>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">The solution includes updates to 3 areas:</font></span></p>  <ul style="margin-bottom: 0in; margin-top: 0in; line-height: normal" type="disc">   <li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 10pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo3"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">New command line startup switch</font></span></li>    <li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 10pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo3"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">New system variables</font></span></li>    <li class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="margin-top: 10pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo3"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">Change load rules for acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp</font></span></li> </ul>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font face="Cambria"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">New Command Line Startup Switch</font></font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">Introduce a new command line switch called “/nolisp”.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">Starting AutoCAD with this switch disables Lisp in AutoCAD (includes LSP, FAS, VLX). This breaks some menu items, express tools, etc. but this is meant for emergency use when a system is infected and the user is afraid of launching AutoCAD.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">NOTE: This startup switch also provides the user the ability to change the AUTOLOAD &amp; AUTOLOADPATH settings. Also, just like other start up switches, this state is only for the current session, and the state is not saved between sessions.</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">(New switch matches naming convention of some existing similar switches such as /nologo, /nohardware, /nossm.)</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">When the “nolisp” command line switch is used, it sets the new LISPENABLED system variable to 0.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">New System Variables </font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us">We added a new read-only sysvar (</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb">LISPENABLED</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us">) which corresponds to the new command line switch. </span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <table class="MsoNormalTable" style="border-collapse: collapse; line-height: normal; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; Also disabled when LISPENABLED=0.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">The checked/unchecked value is still determined by the existing ACADLSPASDOC system variable.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b0192ac46fb86970d-pi"><img title="image" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" border="0" alt="image" src="/assets/image_316210.jpg" width="449" height="219" /></a></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span style="mso-ansi-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-no-proof: yes"></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Changed load rules for acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">Before, we treated acad20xx.lsp and acad20xxdoc.lsp similar to acad.lsp and acaddoc.lsp (i.e. the first file found in the search path is autoloaded). This is no longer the case, we now only load the files found in the Install Support directory.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For example: C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD 2013\Support</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">These files are meant for internal AutoCAD use and the users should not be creating them on their own.</font><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"></b></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD verticals</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">This functionality behaves exactly the same as in AutoCAD. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD for Mac </font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">This functionality behaves nearly identical to AutoCAD for Windows.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in"><i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">NOTE: AutoCAD for Mac supports LSP &amp; FAS files, but not VLX files.</font></span></i><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD LT/AutoCAD OEM</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">This functionality and related system variables are not be available in LT.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>LT doesn’t have this problem because Lisp files cannot be run in AutoCAD LT.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: ; mso-ansi-language: en-us"><font style="font-size: 13pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">The Solution – AutoCAD 2014</font></font></span></h2>  <h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;"><font color="#000000" size="2">Basically, the AutoCAD 2012 SP1 solution was incomplete (it was only limited to Lisp), therefore we needed 2014 Security changes to provide a much more comprehensive barrier to all executable code files that could potentially be malicious.</font></span></h2>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The solution includes updates to the following areas:</font></span></p>  <ul>   <li>Expanding filetypes that are detected by SECURELOAD</li>    <li>Added new settings to Options dialog which correspond to the AUTOLOAD &amp; AUTOLOADPATH sysvars added via the AutoCAD 2012 sp1(now called SECURELOAD &amp; TRUSTEDPATHS)</li>    <li>Split AUTOLOADPATH into 2 sysvars (TRUSTEDPATHS, TRUSTEDDOMAINS)</li>    <li>Implicitly “trust” digitally signed executable files (DLL, EXE, ARX, DBX, etc.)</li>    <li>Define trusted install location for some folders &amp; files</li>    <li>“/safemode” startup switch, SAFEMODE &amp; SAFEMODEAPPS system variables</li>    <li>New warning dialog to warn users when executable files are detected that are not included in TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS</li>    <li>Change Loading for CUIx/MNL files</li>    <li>Add warning message to warn users when writable locations are specified in TRUSTEDPATHS</li>    <li>New LISP function (findtrustedfile)&#160; as opposed to (findfile)</li>    <li>Add new settings to Deployment Wizard     <br /></li> </ul>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">All Filetypes detected by SECURELOAD</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The AUTOLOAD settings introduced in the 2012 sp1 have been updated in 2014 and also expands the type of files we automatically load from the narrow list of user-defined startup files (acad.lsp/fas/vlx, acaddoc.lsp/fas/vlx &amp; acad.dvb) that we targeted in the 2012 sp1 to all ARX, Lisp, .NET assemblies, VBA, Javascript &amp; DLL files.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">In the AutoCAD </span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;">2012 sp1</span><span lang="EN-US">, the AUTOLOAD settings were 0 (Off) and 1 (On).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For AutoCAD 2014, the name of the sysvar changes to SECURELOAD and the values are different (see below).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The AUTOLOAD values are changed from the 2012 SP1, because the “/safemode” startup switch makes the AUTOLOAD =0 (Disabled) setting unnecessary.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If SECURELOAD =1, AutoCAD prompts the user if it tries to load any executable code files (if not located in the Trusted locations and not digitally signed):<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The list of executable file types includes, but is not limited to:</font></span></p>  <ul>   <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">ARX/DBX/CRX </span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">LSP/FAS/VLX/MNL</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">.NET assemblies</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">VBA macros, acad.rx, acVBA.arx, acad.dvb</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">Javascript</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">DLL</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo4"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">SCR files (located on network)</span></font><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></div>   </li> </ul>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">For 2014, we now implicitly “trust” all digitally signed executable files (DLL, EXE, ARX, DBX, etc) - they do not need to be in one of the “Trusted Locations”.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">acad.rx isn’t an executable file, it’s a text-based manifest of references to .arx and .dbx files to be loaded. acad.rx files are just another place AutoCAD looks to find out what executable files it should load (along with the Registry, the Startup Suite, the Autoloader, etc.).</font></span></p>  <table class="MsoNormalTable" style="border-collapse: collapse; line-height: normal; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; mso-padding-alt: 0in 0in 0in 0in" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody>     <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes">       <td style="border-top: windowtext 1pt solid; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Item</font></span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: windowtext 1pt solid; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Description</font></span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 1">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Name</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">SECURELOAD</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 2">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Description</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Controls whether or not AutoCAD autoloads executable files it finds in the regular search path (start-in folder, Drawing folder, Support File Search Path, Install folder)</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 3">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Data Type</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Integer</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 4">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Values</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">0 –Load without warning (Legacy Behavior).</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">1 –Load without warning if the file is also in TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>If not in TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS, display warning dialog before loading.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160; </span>Applies to autoloading &amp; manual loading.</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 9pt">2 –Load without warning if the file is also in TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>If not in TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS, do not display warning dialog.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160; </span>Applies to autoloading &amp; manual loading.</font><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font style="font-size: 9pt">&#160; </font></span></font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">If a file found is not trusted, the command line displays the same error message as selecting “Do Not Load” in the File Loading - Security Concern task dialog.</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">“File load canceled: &lt;path\filename&gt;&quot;</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 5">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Initial Value</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">1</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 6">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; </span>We only “search’ the regular search path, and make trust decisions based on “Trusted locations”.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 3">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Data Type</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Text</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 4">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="504">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Named Profile/Registry</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 7; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt" valign="top" width="174">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 9pt" color="#000000">Accessed from </font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>   </tbody></table>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000" face="Calibri">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Users can specify multiple URLs for Javascript servers.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The URLs support wildcards.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>eg: </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">*.autodesk.com/*<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>// trust anything from Autodesk</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">*.autocadws.com/*<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>// trust anything from AutoCAD WS</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">*.codeplex.com/site/MyProject/*<span style="mso-tab-count: 1">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>// trust anything from a subdomain</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">https://144.111.123.123/*<span style="mso-tab-count: 2">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>// trust only https protocol from a specific IP address</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: "><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#ff0000">&#160;</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Options dialog changes</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">One new branch has been added to the Files tab in the Options dialog (“Trusted Locations”).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>This corresponds to the TRUSTEDPATHS system variable.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The dialog entry is changed from “Trusted File Search Path” to “Trusted Locations”, since we are no longer searching Trusted locations.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Note:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>We are not adding the “Trusted Domain Locations” to the Options dialog (this is only for Deployment).</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt; line-height: 12pt"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">These paths are the designated “trusted sites” for executable code files.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Files in these locations are loaded without prompting (same as legacy behavior).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For that reason, it is recommended that only read-only folders are specified in TRUSTEDPATHS.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial">NOTE: </span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial">A warning message is displayed if user tries to add a writable location.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>See below.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt; line-height: 12pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Trusted Locations</font></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">Users can specify multiple paths.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-fareast-language: ja; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt"><font color="#000000">The tooltip for the new branch is:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Specifies the folders from where AutoCAD can load and execute files that contain code. The AutoCAD executable folder and its subfolders, and the plug-in applications folders are automatically trusted. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt 0.5in; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt"><font color="#000000">Error messages match the existing error messages in the Files tab for folder locations.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For example, if a non-existing folder is specified, an error message is displayed. </font></span><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">NOTE: We support syntax that indicates “trust” for subdirectories of a directory\path.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>‘\…’<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>(three dots) can be used to specify sub-folders.</font></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 13pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt; line-height: 12pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Note:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>We always recursively trust the acad.exe directory and the two Application Plugins folders (but they are not listed).</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 12pt 0in 3pt; line-height: 12pt"><span style="mso-ansi-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-no-proof: yes"></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b0191047dbd18970c-pi"><img title="image" style="border-top: 0px; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If the user selects a writable location for “Trusted Locations”, AutoCAD 2014 presents a warning dialog message with these options...</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; </span>The location specified for “Trusted Locations” is removed, and cursor is left at blank field (same as clicking “Add” button).</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The System tab in Options dialog has also been modified in AutoCAD 2014. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo5"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore">·<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US">The existing “Load acad.lsp with every drawing” checkbox has been moved to a new sub-dialog, and changed from a single checkbox to a pair of radio buttons.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 10pt 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo5"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore">·<span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </span></span></span><span lang="EN-US">A new group box “Security” has been added with a new button “Executable File Settings”.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>This button invokes the new Executable File Settings sub-dialog.</span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The new Executable File Settings dialog allows users to control the loading of executable code files.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span style="mso-ansi-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-no-proof: yes"></span><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b0192ac46fb98970d-pi"><img title="image" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" border="0" alt="image" src="/assets/image_501350.jpg" width="449" height="319" /></a></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">There are three radio buttons<strike> </strike>that correspond to the SECURELOAD system variable.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The existing “Load acad.lsp with every drawing” (ACADLSPASDOC) is changed from a single checkbox to a pair of radio buttons.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The radio buttons for these 2 controls (SECURELOAD, ACADLSPASDOC) are disabled if SAFEMODE=1.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b01901e879058970b-pi"><img title="image" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" border="0" alt="image" src="/assets/image_528479.jpg" width="457" height="351" /></a></p>  <table class="MsoNormalTable" style="border-top: medium none; mso-bidi-font-family: arial; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>   </tbody></table>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The Settings in the Executable File Settings dialog are saved in the AutoCAD Named Profile, in the same Registry location as the AutoCAD Support File Search Path (ACAD), and where we added AUTOLOAD &amp; AUTOLOADPATH in AutoCAD 2012 sp1.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Autodesk\AutoCAD\R19.0\ACAD-B001:409\Profiles\&lt;profilename&gt;\General</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Install Changes </font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The install location for the following files have changed or have been reevaluated:</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">CUIx &amp; MNL files that were previously in the user’s roamable support folder:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>%appdata%\Autodesk\AutoCAD 20xx - &lt;<i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal">lang</i>&gt;\R19.0\enu\Support</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The MNL files have been moved to the localized Support folder of the Install Dir:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>C:\Program Files\Autodesk\AutoCAD 20xx\Support\en-us.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The CUIx files after evaluation are staying in the user’s roamable support folder because they need to be easily edited.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">“/safemode” startup switch</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The /nolisp startup switch introduced in AutoCAD 2012 sp1 has been renamed to ‘/safemode’ and now includes all executable code files. This switch starts AutoCAD in a ‘bare minimum state’ to allow users to change AUTOLOADPATH in Options dialog .i.e. If the ‘/safemode’ startup switch is used when launching AutoCAD, no executable code can be loaded and executed.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Note:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Initially for the /safemode startup switch, we decided to disable all explicit loading of any modules (arx\crx\dbx\lsp\dvb\managed dll, etc), but we found out through testing that this was too restrictive because during AutoCAD’s start up, we explicitly load acmgd.dll, accui.dll and a few others which are necessary for AutoCAD to run.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160; </span>So instead, we added a new read-only hidden sysvar (SAFEMODEAPPS) to designate which modules can be loaded in safemode.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 506.6pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">SAFEMODE</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The LISPENABLED system variable introduced in AutoCAD 2012 sp1 has been renamed to SAFEMODE. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;</span>This sysvar is read-only and is used to determine whether or not AutoCAD was launched in safemode via the “/safemode” startup switch.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <table class="MsoNormalTable" style="border-collapse: collapse; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>   </tbody></table>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#000000" face="Calibri">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>   </tbody></table>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#ff0000" face="Calibri">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">New Warning Dialog - When an executable file is found outside Trusted Locations</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Default setting in the “Executable File Settings” dialog is “Display warning for executable files outside Trusted locations” (SECURELOAD =1).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>When SECURELOAD=1, and AutoCAD tries to load an executable code file from outside of the Trusted locations (Trusted Locations &amp; Trusted Domain Locations) in a non-automation environment, AutoCAD pops up a dialog which warns the user to make sure the file is a trusted file before loading it.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160; </span>The dialog warns the user about loading files from untrusted locations.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">When SECURELOAD=1, this dialog is launched every time AutoCAD detects an executable file that is not in the Trusted Locations.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">When SECURELOAD=0 or 2, this dialog is not displayed.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If more than one executable file is detected outside the Trusted Locations, this dialog displays for each file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If the system does not encounter any of these files outside of the Trusted Locations, then this warning dialog is not displayed.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">When SECURELOAD= 2, AutoCAD does not display a dialog warning, and also does not load executable files found if not listed in Trusted locations.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The command line displays “File load canceled: &lt;path\filename&gt;&quot;.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b0191047dbd2d970c-pi"><img title="image" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" border="0" alt="image" src="/assets/image_306640.jpg" width="391" height="185" /></a></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span style="mso-ansi-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-language: en-gb; mso-no-proof: yes"></span><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">{%pathname%}{%custom_filename%} is a variable field and is populated with the &lt;path/filename&gt; of the detected file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If user picks &quot;Do Not Load&quot;, AutoCAD does NOT continue to look for the file in other directories.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">We cache the “Do Not Load” or “Load” selection for the session, so the next time the user tries to load the same file, we do not prompt again.</font></span></p>  <table class="MsoNormalTable" style="border-top: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-collapse: collapse; border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; line-height: normal; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; mso-padding-alt: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="1"><tbody>     <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes">       <td style="border-top: windowtext 1pt solid; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="142">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">Buttons</font></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: windowtext 1pt solid; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">Closes the dialog and loads the file.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 2">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="142">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in;
