line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">Closes the dialog and does not load the file.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>This is the default option if the user just presses Enter key.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The command line displays an error message.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">Within the APPLOAD dialog, we display:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>&quot;Unable to load &lt;filename&gt; file&quot;</font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 8pt">When loading from the command line (eg: (load &quot;C:/temp/foo.lsp&quot;)), we display:</font><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font style="font-size: 8pt">&#160; </font></span></font></span></p>          <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">&quot;; error: File load canceled: &lt;path\filename&gt;&quot;</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 3">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="142">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">Help</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="532">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 8pt">Opens the Help topic to SECURELOAD.</font><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font style="font-size: 8pt">&#160; </font></span></font></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></b></p>       </td>     </tr>      <tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 4; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">       <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="142">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font style="font-size: 8pt" color="#000000">X or ESC key</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>        <td style="border-top: medium none; border-right: windowtext 1pt solid; border-bottom: windowtext 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-top: 0in; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-left: medium none; padding-right: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" valign="top" width="532">         <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 10pt 0in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 8pt">Closes the dialog and does not load the file.</font><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font style="font-size: 8pt">&#160; </font></span></font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-language: en-us"></span></p>       </td>     </tr>   </tbody></table>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-bidi-language: en-us"><font color="#ff0000" face="Calibri">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">CUIx/MNL Loading changes</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">acad.MNL (MNL files are just LSP files renamed with .MNL extension).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Prior to AutoCAD 2014, MNL files were autoloaded when the corresponding CUI file was loaded. For example, acad.mnl was always loaded when acad.CUIX was loaded. Many of the viruses try to propagate by editing acad.mnl by adding a line in it to load itself.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160; </span></font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">Obviously, this loading style was no longer feasible with the added security. In AutoCAD 2014, we only load the corresponding MNL file if it is found in the TRUSTEDPATHS.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>When a CUIX file is loaded we:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">1.&#160; Check if the path of the CUIX is on the TRUSTEDPATHS. If so, search for the MNL in that directory only.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">2.&#160; If SECURELOAD=1, and if the MNL files are not in Trusted locations, display the File Loading- Security Concern dialog. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US">     <br /><font color="#000000">If SECURELOAD=2, AutoCAD does not display a warning, and also does not load any MNL file found outside the Trusted locations.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000"><font size="2">It is recommended that users put shared CUIx files in a read-only location</font>.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Installer Create Deployment Wizard</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The Create Deployment wizard that you find in the installer has been enhanced to allow a CAD Manager to set these settings while deploying AutoCAD. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;</span>The new settings (same as Executable Code Settings dialog) have been added to the Deployment Wizard Configuration section between the existing Support Content and Search Paths and File Locations sections.</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 12pt"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The new section is called “Executable File Settings”</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The “Trusted Locations” &amp; “Trusted Domain Locations” branches have been added to the existing Search Paths and File Locations section of the Deployment wizard. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: "><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#1f497d">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">LISP function</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">We have added a new lisp function called (findtrustedfile).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>It behaves the same as the existing (findfile) function except that it searches the Trusted Locations (TRUSTEDPATHS).</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD verticals</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">This functionality behaves exactly the same as in AutoCAD. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD OEM 2014</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">This functionality is available in OEM except the following:</font></span></p>  <ul>   <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo6"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">Existing ACADLSPASDOC system variable and related UI is not exposed</span></font></div>   </li>    <li>     <div class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo6"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US"></span></font><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">No changes to Deployment Wizard.</span></font></div>   </li> </ul>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">OEM products have the ability to disable/remove this functionality, including the removal of the system variables and related UI.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD for Mac 2014</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">This functionality is available and behaves nearly identical to AutoCAD for Windows, except there are no UI changes.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The new SECURELOAD, TRUSTEDPATHS &amp; TRUSTEDDOMAINS system variables and the /safemode startup switch is the only way to control the Security settings in AutoCAD for Mac.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">AutoCAD for Mac 2014 has no changes to the Preferences (Options) dialog.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD LT 2014</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">This functionality is not editable in LT.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>LT doesn’t have this problem because Lisp &amp; other executable code files cannot be run in AutoCAD LT.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US">AutoCAD LT hardcodes SECURELOAD=1, and does not expose any of these options in the UI (including the new system variables, Options dialog, or Deployment changes).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Users cannot view or edit the system variables.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Users cannot see the task dialog warning displayed when an executable file attempts to load from outside Trusted Locations (since you can’t load executable code files in AutoCAD LT ), but these code changes are present in AutoCAD LT, just in case there is a way <img class="wlEmoticon wlEmoticon-smile" style="border-top-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-right-style: none" alt="Smile" src="/assets/image_124671.jpg" /></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">The Drawing Feed feature, which utilizes the Javascript API, is present in AutoCAD LT.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">AutoCAD 2014 Javascript API</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font color="#000000">If Javascript is detected from a website outside of Executable Code File Search Path, we display the File Loading- Security Concern dialog.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>
